(HP WorkWise is compatible with Microsoft Windows 10 versions through the Creators Update.)\r\nHP WorkWise is office intelligence rolled into one smartphone app to provide PC security, real-time PC performance updates, and automatic printer driver installation. \r\nNo need to worry if you forgot to lock your PC before leaving your desk. With the HP WorkWise smartphone app, your PC automatically locks and your information is kept secure when your phone gets out of range.
